  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }

  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
      assert Gcd(ai, bi) * 2 <= bi; // From GcdBound
      assert Gcd(ai, bi) <= bi / 2; // divide both sides by 2
      assert Gcd(ai, bi) <= result; // result = n/2 >= bi/2
    }
  }
}

  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{

  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;

    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;

    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }

  decreases c

  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);

  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  // Since a < b, we have a % b == a
  assert a % b == a;
  // Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, b)
  assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, b);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    // In this case, a divides b, so Gcd(b, a) == a
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    // b == a * k
    assert b == a * k;
    // Since b > a and a > 0, k >= 2
    assert k >= 2;
    // Use monotonicity to show a * 2 <= a * k
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    // r is the remainder, 0 < r < a
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    // Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r)
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // r % a == r
    assert r % a == r;
    // Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r)
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // Recursive call
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result

  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  // 1 <= wa < n
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  // wa < wb <= n
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;

  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}
